< review>
Their thin-crust pizzas are really good, and pretty cheap, as far as pizzas go. The crust is crispy and tastes like salted butter, which is very nice. The cheese is less than ideal when it's cold, but you can just microwave it and it'll be no problem. If you're either impatient or don't have access to a microwave, that can be an issue, though.
The pretzel-crust is also quite nice, if I remember correctly. Everything else is okay, but isn't worth it when you can get either a thin-crust or a pretzel-crust instead, in my opinion.</review>

<rating>4</rating><Review>My family and I are new members at this facility.  Prior to joining here, I am an active member at 24 Hour Fitness Pleasanton and San Ramon.  Both 24 Hour Fitness facilities offer similar nice amenities most important for me is a lap pool.  It is kept generally clean and the clientele and staff are also generally nice.

With that said, I cannot make a comparison with Club Sport Pleasanton.  Yes, it is a bit pricey, but what CSP offers is beyond gym access.  First of all, if you have kids, then CSP is a better place.  They have activities centered towards children and a pool facility that is kid friendly.   A Family membership provides you a three-hour time for kids to stay at the Kids' area.   There are two separate areas for younger kids and for the bigger kids.

The place is huge but kept very clean!  Even the men's locker room.   The equipment seems to be good and I love the open spaces they have for stretching, etc.  The wall climbing area inside is a cool feature.  The pools, tennis courts, (lots of it), and basketball courts are nice features as well.  Did I mention that the pool is kept at a nice temperature all year round?

On top of the sports equipment, they have bar areas to relax or even do some work.  Yesterday (July 13th) my wife mentioned that while she was there with our kids, she saw a DJ setting up outdoor and she found out that they have dancing later that evening.  So, really, CSP is not just a gym , it is a health and entertainment facility.  It offers a lifestyle not just a place where you go in and out.

I have not been there a lot yet, so I cannot comment about the staff.  So far, I have not experienced any rude ones as some commented here.  All in all, we love this place and will continue to come here.  The price is actually just right for what they offer and for how well they maintain the areas.

Tennis lessons, swimming lessons, and other classes comes with additional fees but really, the price is not much different and perhaps may be better even when you try to sign-up at lessons offered by the Community parks and recreation centers around.

At this point,  I highly recommend to at least give this place a try.  You will not regret it.<//Review><user_id>114042692694482653419<//user_id><Time>1500062698332< /Time></record></dataset><record>

I've never been to Jiffy Lube, but I saw they would do your oil change while you sat in your vehicle. I pulled of Blackstone into their lot, they guided me to a spot where I waited briefly. They took my info, got me in, changed oil and filter, checked fluids, air pressure and tire condition and helped me set my change oil light.  They were busy, but I was in and out in a reasonable amount of time, and I never had to leave my vehicle and they were all wearing masks.</text>

<text>Really good food and super service. One of the waitresses had a bit of an attitude but the busboy more than made up for it by bringing our dog water, my drinks and the heater. So many other restaurants will defer to the waiter or waitress, but not this kid. He did it all.

As for the food, it ranged from good to great.
Great: oysters were fresh and plump. Truly amazing for the desert. Rubens special and cheesy garlic bread. Shrimp and fish tacos.
Good: The clam chowder. Enjoyed it, just had better.
Needs work: fries - ordered well done, but still not crispy at all. Salsa - they didn‚Äôt have any. Tapatio, Cholula or Tabasco only. Should have ordered extra Poco de Gallo for the tacos, but didn‚Äôt come to mind at the time.

Prices were really good if you order from the lunch menu. Portions might be smaller, but I didn‚Äôt notice and had left overs for dinner.

After reading all the positive reviews, I gave this place a try and was looking forward to having some baked oysters and lobster. Unfortunately, the food was terrible. :( Baked oysters and the spinach were slushy inside and not crispy, and they were tasteless. Garlic bread was a basic cheap baguette and it did not smell garlic. <rating>4< /rating>< Review>
Very solid sea food (mostly) restaurant. Indoor and outdoor seating available. Most entrees in the $20 to $25 range. We had the Green Lip mussels in a very nice garlic wine sauce, mussels seemed very fresh and where large. The crab enchiladas (2) were very good, served with rice and Pico de Gallo. The other dish was was a combination of shrimp, scallops and fish pieces in a red sauce over ziti. Very tasty. Service was decent. Full liquor license.< /Review>

<Text>Long wait, incompetent service, salty dishes. They need more workers, better trained personnel to give better service and organizations.   Food overall is average and inconsistent.

My 5 friends & I heard this place was good from a local waitress.  So we went.  Initially we  were told the wait to be 20 - 30 mins.   It was an hour after we were able to get a table.  This was because they had 4 tables to accommodate 5 - 6 people.  We said it was ok for us to sit at separate smaller tables or saw available two smaller tables and put it together and they said no. They obviously were not accommodating.

It took a while to get the waitress to say hi and 15 mins to get water to the table.

Appetizers came out in good time for artichoke stuffed with crab, Mexican Poke and seafood sampler.  The clam topped with bacon didn't taste fresh.

However main dishes didn't come out until 30 mins after appetizers and only 4/6 dishes.  The other 2 dishes came out 10 mins after!!  Then those two dishes ended up being extremely salty and one of the dishes was reheated.  (Shrimp was over cooked  noodles were very soft (not al dente)).  They offered to replace one of the dishes Rubens special and it came within 5 mins and it was glossy however same saltiness.  So having loss in faith of competence and I didn't want to wait longer; I didn't order more food

The waitress said our order were forgotten.  People who sat down after us gotten their appetizers and main dishes.

The waitress never offered any accommodations while waiting or having salty food.

We all had beer and drinks.  But there was no offer of them or waitress asking if we wanted another one.

In the end the manager gave a discount, however I have lost faith in their ability to produce edible food<//Text>< pics>
